Interjective particles de- noting by the repetition increased abhorrence–as <tam>சிச்சீ</tam>. <tam>சீச்சீ யிங்கிருந் தென்செய்தாய் நெஞ்சமே செத்திலாய்கெடுவாயே</tam>. Fie upon thee, O my heart! what art thou about? at this rate thou wilt perish. (<tam>வைரா</tam>.) <tam>சீபோ</tam>. Time-measure; <tam>தாளம். தண்குரவைச் சீர்</tam> (<tam>புறநா</tam>. 24, 6). 19. Song; <tam>பாட்டு. சேயுய ரூசற்சீர்</tam> (<tam>கலித்</tam>. 131, 24). 20. Metrical foot; <tam>செய்யுளின் ஓருறுப்பு. யாத்தசீரே யடியாப்பெனா</tam> (<tam>தொல். பொ</tam>. 313). 21. Sound of musical instruments; <tam>வாத்தியவோசை. (திவா.)</tam> 22. Sound; <tam>ஓசை. (அக. நி.)</tam> 23. [T. <i>sāre</i>.] See <tam>சீர்சிறப்பு</tam>, 2. <i>Colloq</i>. 24. (Perhaps <tam>காத்தண்டு</tam> mistaken as <tam>காத்தண்டை=காற்றண்டை</tam>.) Tinkling ornaments for the feet; <tam>காலிலணிவதற்கு உரிய தண்டை</tam>. (<smallcap>W</smallcap>.)</p> </blockquote>

		<blockquote><p><hw><tam>சீர்</tam></hw> , <i>s.</i> Beauty, comeliness, fairness, gracefulness, <tam>அழகு</tam>. 2. Prosperity, opulence, wealth, felicity, <tam>வாழ்வு</tam>. 3. Goodness, a good state, or condition, <tam>நன்மை</tam>. 4. Greatness, ex- cellence, moral worth, worthiness, virtue, <tam>நன்னடை</tam>. 5. Distinction, peculiarity, <tam>சிறப்பு</tam>. 6. <i>[vul.]</i> Nature, state, condition, <tam>நிலைமை</tam>. 7. Quality, <tam>தன்மை</tam>. 8. Moderation, consistency, uprightness, sobriety, deco- rum, propriety of character or deportment, <tam>கிரமம்</tam>. <i>(c.)</i> 9. Reputation, renown, fame, celebrity, <tam>புகழ்</tam>. 10. A picture; fancy work, <tam>சித்திரம்</tam>. 11. Weight, gravity, <tam>பாரம்</tam>. 12. The scales of a balance, <tam>தராசு</tam>. 13. Libra of the Zodiac, <tam>துலாராசி</tam>. 14. A foot in poetry, <tam>செய்யுளுறுப்பிலொன்று</tam>. 15. Tune in music, <tam>தாளவொத்து</tam>. 16. Tinkling ornaments for the feet, <tam>காற்றண்டை</tam>. 17. A club, a bludgeon, <tam>தண்டாயுதம்</tam>. (<tam>சது</tam>.) 18. A pole for the should- er in carrying burdens, <tam>காவுதடி</tam>. (<tam>நிக</tam>.) 19. Gold, <tam>பொன்</tam>. 20. Noise, sound, <tam>ஒலி</tam>. 21. Wielding the shield as a fencer, <tam>சிலம்பம்</tam>. The metrical feet are thirty, divided into five classes, viz.: 1. <tam>உரிச்சீர்</tam>, or <tam>ஆசிரியவுரிச்சீர்</tam>, feet peculiar to the <tam>அகவல்</tam> verse–as <i>(a.)</i> <tam>தேமா</tam>, foot of two simple syllables, a spondee. <i>(b.)</i> <tam>புளிமா</tam>, one compound and one simple syllable; an iambus. <i>(c.)</i> <tam>கருவிளம்</tam>. Two compound syllables, a pyrrhic. <i>(d.)</i> <tam>கூவிளம்</tam>. One simple and one compound syllable, a trochee. The names serve also as models for the kinds of feet respectively. They are names of trees and their fruits. 2. <tam>வெண்சீர்</tam>, or <tam>வெண்பாஉரிச்சீர்</tam>. Feet peculiar to <tam>வெண்பா</tam> verse; as <i>(a.)</i> <tam>தே</tam>-<tam>மாங்</tam>-<tam>காய்</tam>. A foot of three simple sylla- bles. <i>(b.)</i> <tam>புளி</tam>-<tam>மாங்</tam>-<tam>காய்</tam>. One compound and two simples. <i>(c.)</i> <tam>கரு</tam>-<tam>விளங்</tam>–<tam>காய்</tam>. Two compounds and one simple; an anapæst. <i>(d.)</i> <tam>கூ</tam>-<tam>விளங்</tam>-<tam>காய்</tam>. A simple, a compound and a simple. 3. <tam>வஞ்சியுரிச்சீர்</tam>, or <tam>வஞ்சிச்சீர்</tam>. Feet peculiar to <tam>வஞ்சி</tam> verse; as <i>(a.)</i> <tam>தே</tam>-<tam>மாங்</tam> -<tam>கனி</tam>. A foot of two simple syllables and one compound. <i>(b.)</i> <tam>புளி</tam>-<tam>மாங்</tam>-<tam>கனி</tam>. One compound, one simple, and one compound; an amphibrach. <i>(c.)</i> <tam>கரு</tam>-<tam>விளங்</tam>- <tam>கனி</tam>. Three compounds, a tribrach. <i>(d.)</i> <tam>கூ</tam>- <tam>விளங்</tam>-<tam>கனி</tam>. One simple and two compound syllables. 4. <tam>பொதுச்சீர்</tam>. Feet of four syllables peculiar to <tam>வஞ்சி</tam> verse; there are sixteen of them; the models for these are formed by adding respectively, <tam>தண்</tam>-<tam>ணிழல்</tam>, <tam>தண்</tam>-<tam>பூ</tam>, <tam>நறும்</tam>-<tam>பூ</tam>, <tam>நறு</tam>-<tam>நிழல்</tam> to the terms em- ployed in the <tam>உரிச்சீர்</tam>. 5. <tam>ஓரசைச்சீர்</tam>. A foot of a single syllable; as <i>(a.)</i> <tam>நாள்</tam>. A foot of one simple syllable. <i>(b.)</i> <tam>மலர்</tam>. A foot of a compound syllable.–<i>Note.</i> 1. One use of the last two is to end the <tam>வெண்பா</tam> verse. –<i>Note.</i> 2. Sometimes feet answering to <tam>காசு</tam>, instead of <tam>நாள்</tam>, and <tam>பிறப்பு</tam> instead of <tam>மலர்</tam>, are employed to end the <tam>வெண்பா</tam> verse, i. e., the addition of <tam>குற்றுகரம்</tam> or short <tam>உ</tam> to the foregoing; and rarely the full <tam>உ</tam>, or <tam>முற்றுகரம்</tam> is found. <tam>சீராயிருக்கிறேன்</tam>. I am in a good state. <p2><tam>சீரழிக்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To disturb, subvert, per- vert. 2. To ruin, demolish. 3. To disparage one's character. <i>(c.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>சீராக</tam>, <i>inf. 		from <a href="/dictionaries/winslow/">Winslow's <i>"A comprehensive Tamil and English dictionary"</i></a>

The sentient soul; according to the Vedantic system, the emanation of the deity incorporated with the body, giving it life, motion and sensation; hence also called, <tam>சீவாத்துமா</tam>. It is opposed to the abstract state of the soul, or as identified with deity, <tam>பரமாத்துமா</tam>.–<i>Note.</i> According to the Agamas, the soul is eter- nal, but destined to obsorption in the deity, which is the ultimate object in view in furnishing it with bodies, and with various means for its illumination. 3. A living being, an animal, <tam>சீவசெந்து</tam>. 4. A name of Jupiter, <tam>வியாழம்</tam>. 5. A magnet, <tam>காந்தம்</tam>. <i>(R.)</i> 6. <i>(fig.)</i> Energy, spirit, life, animation, <tam>முயற்சி</tam>–used in the negative form. W. p. 351. <smallcaps>JEEVA.</smallcaps> <tam>சீவனும்பிராணனுமாயிருக்கிறார்கள்</tam>. They are closely united, <i>(lit.)</i> as the life and the vital airs. <tam>சீவன்வந்தது</tam>. Life is restored–spoken of one whose fears are banished. <tam>நடக்கச்சீவனில்லை</tam>. Not life enough to walk. <tam>படிப்போடேசீவனைவிடுகிறான்</tam>. He spends his life in learning. <tam>ஏனக்குப்பசியினாற்சீவன்போகிறது</tam>. I am ready to die of hunger. <p2><tam>சீவனுண்டாய்ப்பேச</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To speak aloud.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவனைக்கொடுக்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To impart life. 2. To prolong life–as pretended by one possessed. 3. To sacrifice one's life for another. 4. To save one from ruin, by giving the means of subsistence. 5. To inspire one with courage, <tam>தைரியப்படுத்த</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவனைமாய்த்துக்கொள்ள</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To commit suicide, to lay violent hands on one's self.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவனைவாங்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To take away life. 2. <i>(fig.)</i> To put one to great hard- ships.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவனோடிருக்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To be alive, to live.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவனோடுகூடியகாரியம்</tam>, <i>s. [prov.] (in di- vination.)</i> A question, or matter con- nected with life, or with a living being. 2. A thing of vital importance.</p2> <p2><tam>கிழட்டுச்சீவன்</tam>–<tam>கிழச்சீவன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> An old person, man or woman.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவன்முத்தன்</tam>, <i>s. (in Agama phil.)</i> The soul freed from <tam>பாசம்</tam> before the death of the body, and no longer subject to births. (<tam>சிவ</tam>. <tam>போ</tam>.)</p2></p> </blockquote>

From the ant to the elephant, there are 8,400,000 species of living creatures.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவநாசம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Something detrimental to life.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவந்தன்</tam>, <i>s. [loc.]</i> One who is alive.</p2> <p2><tam>சீவரட்சை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Preservation of life–as by the divine being, or by a benevo- lent person in famine, &c. 2. <script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/jquery-3.2.1.min.js"></script>
<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/popper.min.js"></script>
<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/bootstrap.min.js"></script>

<script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        $(document).keypress(function(event) {
                var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keycode == "116") {
                        var selection = window.getSelection().toString();
			var q_param = $.trim(selection);
			q_param = q_param.replace(/[;]/g, '%3B');
			var q_param = q_param.replace(/\/?#/g,'')
			//console.log(selection)
			//console.log(q_param)
			var q_url = 'tamil/get_transliteration.py?q=' + q_param;
			$.ajax({
				url:q_url,
				dataType: "text"
			}).done(function(data){
				//console.log(data)
				var title_text = selection.replace(/\u00a0\u00a0/g,'\u00a0') 
				title_text = title_text.replace(/\u00a0/g,'<br/>')
				var title = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">Transliteration for: ' + title_text + '</span>';
				var display_data = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">' + data + '</span>';
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').html(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').html(display_data);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			}).fail(function(xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
				console.log(xhr)
				console.log(ajaxOptions)
				console.log(thrownError)
				if (thrownError === 'Request-URI Too Long') {
					var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				}
				else if (thrownError === 'Internal Server Error') {
					var message = "The transliteration code encountered a problem. Please try again.";
				}
				var title = "Error: " + thrownError;
				//var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').text(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').text(message);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			});
                };
        });
    });

</script>
